    Si Qi Decoction: This remedy treats phlegm caused by emotional distress, which may feel like a plum pit lodged in the throat, cause phlegm and qi stagnation in the middle, induce phlegm obstruction leading to shortness of breath, or result in phlegm and fluid accumulation causing nausea and vomiting. It also treats those with phlegm in abnormal discharge. Ingredients include: 1.5 qian of processed Pinellia, fresh Perilla leaves, processed Magnolia bark, and 1 qian of Poria, all simmered with ginger and jujube water.

    Clove and Gelatin Decoction: This remedy treats persistent uterine bleeding and abundance of thick, white discharge, similar to a leaky roof with occasional fresh blood. Patients often feel cold below the navel and seek clothing for warmth, with a pulse that is sometimes slightly rapid. Ingredients include: 0.3 qian each of cooked Rehmannia and white peony, 0.4 qian each of Chuanxiong and clove, 0.6 qian of donkey-hide gelatin, 1 qian of fresh mugwort leaves, and 1.2 qian of Angelica sinensis. The Chuanxiong is finely ground, while the Angelica is washed with wine and chopped. The cooked Rehmannia and clove are also finely ground, with mugwort chopped. All are combined, boiled with 5 large cups of water down to 1.2 cups, strained, then gelatin is added and simmered until the volume is reduced to 1 cup, taken warm on an empty stomach.

    Yan Hu Ku Lian Decoction: This remedy treats cold, cramping pain below the navel, with extreme cold, and white discharge. Ingredients include: 0.1 qian of Coptis, 0.2 qian each of Corydalis and Ku Lian Zi, 0.3 qian each of prepared Aconite and cinnamon, and 0.5 qian of honey-fried licorice, along with 1 qian of cooked Rehmannia. All ingredients are combined and boiled with 3 large cups of water down to 1 cup, taken before meals.[46p]

    　　神圣复气汤　治复气乘冬，足太阳寒气、足少阴肾水之旺。能令母实，手太阴肺实，反来侮土，火木受邪，腰背胸膈，闭塞疼痛，善嚏，口中涎，目中泣，鼻中流浊涕不止；或如息肉不闻香臭，咳嗽痰沫，上热如火，下寒如冰，头作阵痛，目中流火，视物(目巟)(目巟)，耳鸣耳聋，头并口鼻或恶风寒，喜日阳，夜卧不安，常觉痰塞，膈咽不通，口失味，两胁缩急而痛，牙齿动摇，不能嚼物，阴汗，前阴冷，行步敧侧，起居艰难，掌中寒，风痹麻木，小便数而昼多，夜频而欠，气短喘喝，少气不足以息，卒遗失无度，妇人白带，阴户中大痛，牵心而痛，黧黑失色，男子控睪牵心腹阴阴而痛，面如赭色，食少，大小便不调，心烦霍乱，逆气里急，而腹皮色白，后出余气，腹不能努，或肠鸣，膝下筋急，肩胛大痛，此皆寒水来复火土之雠也。[47p]

    Shen Sheng Fu Qi Decoction treats the resurgence of qi in winter, affected by the cold of the foot yang and the thriving water of the foot shao yin kidney. It can invigorate the mother, strengthen the hand tai yin lung, and counter the excess of earth, leading to imbalances where fire and wood suffer from pathogens. All these are due to the encroachment of cold water reviving the fires of earth.[47p]

    Black fuzi and dried ginger, three parts each. Six parts of angelica root. For wind prevention, soak the seeds of the (wood) nut, remove the skin and tip, then grind to a paste. Five parts of ginseng. Soak pinellia in water seven times. Seven parts each of chuan shengma. Five parts each of white chrysanthemum and dried tangerine peel. Two parts of fresh rehmannia, washed with wine. Three parts each of coptis soaked in yellow wine and phellodendron soaked in yellow wine. Soak the above four ingredients in new water for one day. Two parts of xinxi. Three parts each of chuanxiong finely ground and manjingzi. Soak the above three ingredients in new water for half a large cup for one day.

    Combine all thirteen ingredients, including white chrysanthemum, into one dose, using five cups of water. Boil down to two cups, then add the three ingredients of tangerine peel and others, further boil down to one cup. Next, add fresh rehmannia and the seven ingredients, then simmer until reduced to one large cup. Strain, slightly warm, and take on an empty stomach. Avoid meat soup; meat is acceptable but does not support the fire of the meridians.[48p]

    Chuanbi Xiang: Treats prolonged cold in the uterus, with red and white discharges.

    Another formula for treating women's red and white discharges:
    Ping Wei San: Roast Yellow Qi, divided into two parts as appropriate. Mix and take.

    Shi Zao Tang: Treats heat stagnation from discharges that do not disperse.

    Gua Di San: Treats red and white discharges, adjusting use as appropriate. Contains seventy-five seeds of Gua Di and red small beans, half a tael each of Ren Shen and Gan Cao, ground into fine powder. Take one qian, half, or two qian according to deficiency and excess, mixed with juice on an empty stomach. One formula has two taels and five fen of Gan Cao.[49p]

    For treatment, the same as above.
    The gourd stalk does not limit the amount.
    Prepare a fine powder to the right. Take one or two coins each time, mixed with the juice of fresh vegetables. For flank pain, add whole scorpion. For headaches, add gardenia.

    Daoshui Wan
    For treatment, the same as above.
    Two taels of rhubarb and skullcap, four taels of talcum powder and black morning glory head powder. Prepare a fine powder, form into pills the size of a wutong nut, take fifty pills each time, or increase to a hundred, taken with warm water before bed.

    Yugong San
    For treatment, the same as above.
    Four taels of black morning glory head powder, one tael of fennel (stir-fried), or add one tael of wood fragrance. Prepare a fine powder, mix one or two coins with natural juice of fresh ginger, and take before bed.

    Wuyou San
    For treatment, the same as above.
    One tael each of astragalus, muxiang, mulberry bark, and dried tangerine peel; half a tael each of pepper, white atractylodes, and wood fragrance; four taels of morning glory head powder. Prepare a fine powder, take three to five coins mixed with natural juice of fresh ginger after meals.

    Wuling San
    For treatment, the same as above.
    Half a tael each of cinnamon, alisma, poria, white atractylodes, and prepare a fine powder. Take two coins mixed with hot soup or fresh water.

    Jade Candle Powder (same as Danxi) treats red and white vaginal discharge; adjust the dosage as needed. Angelica, Peony, Chuanxiong, cooked Rehmannia, Glauber's salt, rhubarb, and Licorice. The above should be chewed and then decocted with three slices of ginger.

    Three Flower Divine Protector Pills treat red and white vaginal discharge; adjust based on symptoms. Light powder one qian; rhubarb one liang; Qian Niu Zi two liang; ground Euphorbia paniculata, Licorice, and Euphorbia each half a liang. The above should be powdered, formed into pills the size of a small bean; initially take five pills, then increase by five for each subsequent dose, swallowed with warm water three times a day.

    Small Stomach Pill treats the same as above.

    Euphorbia paniculata is mixed evenly, placed in a tiled container overnight, stirred continuously while frying until black but not burnt. Licorice is wrapped in flour, soaked in flowing water for half a day, washed and dried in the sun, winter seven days, spring and autumn five days, summer one day. Euphorbia is boiled in flowing water for one hour, then washed and dried, each half a liang. Rhubarb is wrapped in wet paper and stewed without burning, cut and dry-fried with wine until dry, one and a half liang; Huangbai three liang, fried. The above should be powdered, made into pills the size of sesame seeds. Take twenty to thirty pills each time, swallowing with saliva before bed, or with a sip of clear soup to dispel damp heat and phlegm accumulation in the diaphragm. For better results, take on an empty stomach.[51p]

    Five Accumulated Dispersals
    Half summer (Pinellia) - 2 parts
    White atractylodes - 3 parts
    Chuanxiong (Szechuan lovage) - 3 parts
    Peony - 3 parts
    Licorice - 3 parts
    Poria - 3 parts
    Angelica - 3 parts
    Cinnamon - 3 parts
    Dried orange peel - 6 parts
    Ephedra - 6 parts
    Magnolia bark - 4 parts
    Dried ginger - 4 parts
    Platycodon - 1.5 parts
    Atractylodes - 7.5 parts
    Bitter orange peel - 5 parts

    Boil these with ginger and scallions for oral consumption. If regulating menstruation, add mugwort and vinegar. If the body is thin and has sweating, remove atractylodes and ephedra.

    Pingwei Powder
    For women with vaginal discharge, this supplements the protective qi and strengthens the spleen.
    Atractylodes - 2 qian (a traditional unit of weight)
    Dried orange peel - 1 qian and 4 fen (1 qian = 10 fen)
    Magnolia bark, with ginger juice, roasted - 1 qian
    Licorice - 8 fen

    Boil with ginger and jujube, adding a little salt for warm oral consumption.

    Erchen Decoction
    For treating phlegm-damp in overweight individuals leading to excessive white discharge.
    Half summer - 1 qian
    Dried orange peel - 2 qian
    Poria - 8 fen
    Licorice - 4 fen

    Add three slices of fresh ginger and boil for oral consumption. If there is blood deficiency, combine with Four Substance Decoction. If there is qi deficiency, combine with Four Gentlemen Decoction.[52p]

    Huangqi Jianzhong Decoction treats white discharge resembling mucus, with a strong fishy odor. Ingredients: Huangqi and Cinnamon each 0.7 grams, Licorice 1.5 grams, Bai Shao 3 grams.     Dayan Huo Suo Powder is used for women with damp-heat causing leucorrhea.     Ingredients: Huang Qin, Bai Zhu - each 9 grams; Huang Bo - 4.5 grams; Chopi, Bai Shao, Shan Zhu Yu - each 7.5 grams; Bai Zhi, Huang Lian - each 6 grams.

    Cang Bo Xin Xiong Powder: Treats women with upper symptoms of headache and nasal discharge, and lower symptoms of leucorrhea.
    Ingredients: Cang Zhu, Huang Bo, Xin Yi, Chuan Xiong, Nan Xing, Hua Shi, Ban Xia, Mu Li, Huang Qin (wine-fried) - all equal amounts.
    Prepare by decocting in water and take warm.

    Gui Bo Jiang Zhi Pill: Treats red or white leucorrhea, sometimes with abdominal pain.
    Ingredients: Gui Ban - 450 grams; Huang Bo - 60 grams; Shan Zhi Zi (fried) - 7.5 grams; Gan Jiang (fried) - 3 grams.
    Prepare as a powder, mix with wine to form pills, and take with warm water.

    Ce Bai Chopi Pill: Treats emotional distress leading to rapid pulse and leucorrhea.
    Ingredients: Chopi - 600 grams; Ce Bai Ye, Huang Bo (wine-steamed), Huang Lian - each 25 grams; Xiang Fu, Bai Zhu, Bai Shao - each 30 grams; Bai Zhi (burned for char) - 15 grams.
    Prepare as a powder, mix with congee to form pills, and take with rice drink.

    Prepare as a powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of wutong seeds, about 50-60 pills, take with warm water. If in summer, omit ginger and add Hua Shi.[54p]

    Women's Vaginal Discharge Medicines

    Xiao Wujiji Pill - Treats foul-smelling discharge, abdominal pain, and coldness in the lower body. Ingredients include: Wu Zhu Yu (1 tael), Liang Jiang (1 tael), Bai Jiang (1 tael), Dong Gui (1 tael), Shao Yao (1 tael), Yan Hu Suo (1 tael), Bu Gu Zhi (1 tael), Chen Pi (1 tael), Chuan Jiao (1 tael), Qing Pi (1 tael), Liu Ji Nu (1 tael), Sheng Di (1 tael), E Zhu (1 tael), Chuan Xiong (1 tael), He Ye Hui (4 taels), Bei Ai (2 taels), and Black Chicken Meat. Grind the ingredients into powder, stew with black chicken meat to form pills. Each dosage consists of 50 pills. For a simple case of red discharge, consume with clear tea.

    Qin Zhu Shao Kui Pill - Treats phlegm-related white discharge. Ingredients include: Bai Zhu (2 taels), Huang Qin (5 qian), Red and White Cosmos Flower (2.5 qian), Shao Yao (7.5 qian). Grind into powder, steam into pills, then take with Si Wu Decoction.

    Amber Cinnabar Pill - Treats discharge in young women. Ingredients include: Amber (4 qian), Mu Xiang (4 qian), Dong Gui (4 qian), Myrrh (4 qian), Frankincense (1 qian), Musk (2.5 fen), and Cinnabar (2.5 fen). Grind into powder, form into water pills the size of longan seeds. Take one pill with warm wine.

    Yimucao Paste - Treats postpartum red and white discharge. Collect Yimucao with purple flowers on the Dragon Boat Festival, clean the roots thoroughly. Pound in a stone mortar, strain the thick juice through cloth, and simmer in a sand pot over even fire until it turns to a paste akin to the color of brown sugar. Store in a ceramic jar, taking one spoonful mixed with gelatinized wormwood soup. Another method is to dry and grind into powder, avoiding iron. Form into honey pills the size of small pellets, taking one with gelatinized wormwood soup.[55p]

    Four Gentlemen Decoction: For women with leucorrhea and extremely weak spleen and stomach, use this formula with modifications.

    • Bai Zhu: 2 qian
    • Fu Ling: 2 qian
    • Licorice: 6 fen
    • Fresh Ginger: 3 slices
    • Jujube: 1 piece

    • White Peony: 2.5 qian
    • Rehmannia: 2.5 qian
    • Angelica: 2 qian
    • Chuanxiong: 2 qian
      Boil and take.

    • Cinnamon Branch: 3 qian
    • White Peony: 3 qian
    • Licorice: 1 qian
      Boil with ginger and jujube and take.

    Regulating Middle Decoction: An ancient formula for leucorrhea, can be used with modifications to dry dampness and strengthen the spleen.

    • Licorice: 1.5 qian
    • Ginseng: 2 qian
    • Bai Zhu: 2 qian
    • Dried Ginger (processed): 2 qian
      Boil with ginger and jujube and take.

    Shengyang Tiao Jing Decoction: Treats summer menstrual disorders, such as excessive discharge, fatigue from diet and labor, and persistent bleeding. Ingredients: 0.5 qian of Angelica pubescens, 0.7 qian of Vitex negundo, 1 qian each of Angelica sinensis, Saposhnikovia divaricata, Glycyrrhiza uralensis, and Cimicifuga, and 1.5 qian each of Bupleurum, Notopterygium incisum, Atractylodes macrocephala, and Astragalus membranaceus. Take this with water on an empty stomach, pressing with food.

    Banxia Pill: An ancient formula for treating discharge, with modifications to dry dampness and strengthen the spleen. Prepared by stir-frying pinellia with fragrant oil, grind into a powder, make into pills the size of a jujube, taking 30 to 50 pills with ginger decoction.

    Weifeng Decoction: Treats wind evil harming the kidneys, causing discharge resembling black blood. Ingredients: 0.7 qian each of Poria cocos, Ginseng, Angelica sinensis, Chuanxiong, Atractylodes macrocephala, Peony, and Cinnamon. Add 100 grains of millet. Prepare and take warm.

    Bujing Gu Zhen Decoction: Also known as Buyang Gu Zhen Decoction. Treats long-standing issues of continuous bleeding and persistent white discharge. Ingredients: 1 qian each of Bupleurum, Scutellaria baicalensis, (wood-fragrant) apricot kernel, and Glycyrrhiza uralensis; 2 qian each of Ginseng and dried ginger; 0.5 qian of orange peel; and 1 whole white sunflower bloom. Take this warm. If treating red discharge, use red sunflower. Another formula uses 16 white sunflower blooms.[57p]

    　　四炒固真丹　治妇人崩带下血，子宫血海虚冷等证。　　苍朮一斤，分作四分：一分用茴香、青盐各一两炒，一分用川乌、川楝各一两炒；一分用川椒、破故纸各一两炒，一分用酒酢炒。俱以朮黄为度，去各炒药　　右将各炒药为末，煮药，酒酢打糊，丸梧子大，每服三十丸，淡酢汤下。
    　　清白散 【《医鉴》，下同】 　治白带。　　当归　川芎　白芍炒　生地酒洗过姜汁炒　黄蘗盐水炒　贝母　樗根白皮酒炒，各等分　干姜炒黑　甘草各减半　　右銼，一剂，生姜煎服。如肥人多湿痰，加白朮、半夏。如赤带，加酒芩、荆芥。久下，加熟地、牡蛎。如气虚，加人参、黄芪。如腰腿痛，加鹿角胶，或只以二陈汤加苍朮、白朮。如血虚，加芎归。如升膀胱之湿，二陈加升麻、柴胡、苍朮、白朮。[58p]

    Sichao Guozhen Dan

    This treats women's conditions such as excessive uterine bleeding or discharge of blood, as well as symptoms of a cold and empty uterine blood sea.

    Ingredients:

    • 1 pound of Atractylodes: divided into four parts
      • One part mixed with 1 tael each of fennel and Qing salt and stir-fried
      • One part mixed with 1 tael each of Chuanwu and Chuanlian and stir-fried
      • One part mixed with 1 tael each of Chuan pepper and Poge paper and stir-fried
      • One part stir-fried with wine vinegar

    Use Atractylodes as a measure for each stir-fried ingredient. Remove each stir-fried herb.

    Grind all the stir-fried ingredients into a powder, boil the herbs, and mix them into a paste with wine vinegar. Form into pills the size of Chinese walnuts. Take 30 pills each time with diluted vinegar soup.

    Qingbai San

    This treats white discharge.

    Ingredients:

    • Angelica Sinensis (Dang Gui)
    • Chuanxiong
    • White Peony (Bai Shao), stir-fried
    • Fresh Rehmannia (Sheng Di), washed with wine and stir-fried
    • Berberine (Huangbo), stir-fried with salt water
    • Fritillaria (Bei Mu)
    • Ailanthus bark (Chu Gen), white skin, stir-fried with wine, all in equal amounts
    • Dried Ginger, stir-fried until dark
    • Licorice, halved

    Grind together to make one dose, decoct with fresh ginger and take.

    For overweight individuals with damp phlegm, add Atractylodes and Banxia. For red discharge, add wine-fried Scutellaria and Jing Jie. For long-term discharge, add cooked Rehmannia and oyster. For qi deficiency, add ginseng and Astragalus. For lower back and leg pain, add deer antler glue or just use Erchen Decoction with Atractylodes and Bai Zhu. For blood deficiency, add Chuanxiong and Dang Gui. For dampness rising to the bladder, add to Erchen Decoction with Shengma, Chaihu, Atractylodes, and Bai Zhu.[58p]

    　　解带散　治妇人血气不调，湿热白带，四肢倦怠，五心烦热，痰郁嘈杂。　　归身一钱半　白芍酒炒　白朮炒，各一钱二分　苍朮米泔浸炒　茯苓　香附酢炒　丹皮酒洗　陈皮去白，各一钱　甘草炙，四分　延胡炒　川芎各八分　　右銼，一剂，生姜煎，空心服。

    Four Spirit Pill treats leucorrhea.
    Use eight taels of sweet cumin, soak two taels each in wine and vinegar and children's urine for three days, then stir-fry. Stir-fry cardamom after removing the shell, and prepare wheat bran-soaked Atractylodes. Stir-fry crushed oyster shells mixed with two taels each of white peony root and honey water. Grind the above into powder, and make pills the size of a walnut, taking fifty to sixty pills at a time with empty stomach and yellow wine.

    Two Qi Pill treats red and white discharge.
    Melt bulk sulfur, pouring it into water seven times. Add one tael each of cinnabar, cassia, and dried ginger. Use five qian of processed Aconite, removing the skin, and add two taels of deer antler, plus one qian of musk, processed with vinegar. Grind into powder, form into pills the size of a walnut, and take thirty pills at a time with empty stomach and salt water. If there are symptoms of weakness and fever, first take four medicines soup four qian, and Xiao Chai Hu decoction six qian, then combine with Shiquan Dabu decoction.

    Another prescription for women with red and white discharge with upper heat and lower cold complaints, bad breath, dry throat, toothache, tinnitus, upper and lower pain, fever with aversion to cold, sour reflux, nausea, abdominal pain, mixed colors in discharge without regularity, pale face and thin body, lack of appetite:
    Use Angelica, Chuanxiong, red peony, raw land, dried tangerine peel, fried half summer ginger, Atractylodes with wheat bran, soaked and stir-fried Cangzhu, sweet cumin soaked in children's urine and stir-fried, Chaihu, Shengma, yellow qin stir-fried in wine, Danpi, and licorice. Grind the above, and take it with boiled ginger. One prescription adds Yeyu for better results.[61p]

    　　下熏药 【《治法汇》】 　治脐下寒痛如冰。　　三柰　川乌　大椒各五分　全蝎三个　柴胡　羌活各二钱　白矾枯，三分　升麻二分　大蒜　破故纸与蒜同焙，各一钱麝少许　　右为末，炼蜜丸弹子大，绵裹，留系在阴外，内阴中。
    　　导痰丸 【《元珠方》】 　带下有痰者兼服此。　　廿遂制　百药煎各二两　全蝎　僵蚕各一两　大半夏六两，分作三分：一分用白矾一两为末浸水；一分用肥皂角为末浸水，一分用巴豆肉一百粒为末浸水。余药在下半夏在上，浸至十日或半月，要常动水令二药相透，次相合处拣去巴豆并皂角，将余水以余火煮令水干，取出半夏切，捣碎晒干，或阴干亦佳　　右为细末，薄糊丸如梧子大，每服十丸或十五丸，亦量人虚实，白汤下。[62p]

    Xia Xun Yao: For treating cold pain below the navel as if frozen. Combine three parts of San Nai, five parts each of Chuan Wu and Da Jiao, three pieces of Quan Xie, two qian each of Chai Hu and Qiang Huo, three parts of burnt Bai Fan, two parts of Sheng Ma, one qian each of Da Suan and Po Gu Zhi, both roasted together, and a small amount of musk. Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey into pills the size of a marble, wrap in cotton, and keep attached to the exterior of the lower abdomen.

    Dao Tan Wan: For those with phlegm in the lower discharge, take this in addition. Prepare twenty doses: each herb boiled in two liang, one liang each of Quan Xie and Jiang Can, and six liang of half summer, divided into three parts: one part treated with one liang of Bai Fan, another part with soap pod, and the last part with one hundred seeds of Ba Dou, all soaked in water. The remaining herbs are on top of the half summer. Soak for ten days to half a month, stirring regularly to ensure the herbs mix well; then remove the Ba Dou and soap pod. Boil the remaining water until reduced, extract the half summer, chop it, crush it, and dry it either in the sun or in the shade. This will yield a fine powder, which can be formed into thin pills the size of a wooden nut. Take ten or fifteen pills, adjusted according to one's condition, with warm water.[62p]

    　　万灵膏药 【《医贯》】 　治元气虚弱，女人赤白带下，子宫虚冷，血山崩等证，贴丹田，熨一百二十手。　　香油四斤　白芷　赤芍　大黄　黄连　白芍　两头尖　草乌　元参　川芎　生地　川椒　胎发头生男者　穿山甲　熟地　杏仁　槐角　黄蘗各一两　归尾二两　木鳖子五十个，去壳　黄香十二两，化开，倾米泔水九次　萞麻子去壳　巴豆各一百二十粒，去壳　　以上各咀片，入油内浸，春五日、夏三日、秋七日、冬十日，取倾锅内，熬枯黑色，滤去滓，将净油入锅，文武火熬，滴水成珠，方细退火，黄丹二斤飞过焙干，徐徐下，以槐柳桃杏楮各二枝，不住手搅，再下黄香，　　去火少冷，又下后细药搅匀，将好瓶贮之，放水内浸一七，出火气，用时放滚水内，顿化摊开。细药列后：阿魏　丁香　沉香各一两　麝香二两　血竭　孩儿茶　乳香　没药各三两　珍珠制，五钱　琥珀三钱　　右各为极细末，入前膏内。[63p]

    Ten Thousand Spirits Ointment
    (from "Yiguan")
    To treat symptoms of weak vitality, women's red and white discharge, coldness in the uterus, and blood disorders, apply to the lower abdomen and massage one hundred and twenty times.

    Ingredients:
    4 pounds of sesame oil
    1 ounce each of:

    • Bai Zhi (Angelica dahurica)
    • Chi Shao (Red Peony)
    • Da Huang (Rhubarb)
    • Huang Lian (Coptis)
    • Bai Shao (White Peony)
    • Liang Tou Jian (Two-Headed Sharp)
    • Cao Wu (Wild Aconite)
    • Yuan Shen (Scrophularia)
    • Chuan Xiong (Ligusticum wallichii)
    • Sheng Di (Rehmannia)
    • Chuan Jiao (Sichuan Pepper)
    • Hair from the first-born male
    • Chuan Shan Jia (Pangolin)
    • Shu Di (Cooked Rehmannia)
    • Xing Ren (Apricot Kernel)
    • Huai Jiao (Sophora)
    • Huang Bai (Phellodendron)

    2 ounces of Gui Wei (Rehmannia root tails)
    50 pieces of Mu Bie Zi (Trichosanthes) shelled
    12 ounces of Huang Xiang (Saffron)
    Soaked in rice wash nine times
    Shell and prepare:

    • Bai Dou (Physalis) and Ba Dou (Croton) — each 120 seeds, shelled

    All the above are to be sliced and soaked in oil.
    During spring for five days, summer for three days, autumn for seven days, and winter for ten days, strain and simmer until dark and thick, then filter out the residue, returning the oil to the pot. Boil over gentle heat until it forms droplets, then reduce heat further. Add 2 pounds of Yellow Dan (Lead Sulfide) that has been dried, stirring continuously with branches from Sophora, willow, peach, apricot, and paper mulberry—each two branches—until well mixed. Add Huang Xiang, let cool slightly, then mix in fine powders thoroughly before transferring to a suitable bottle, soaking in water for seven days to reduce heat. When ready to use, place in boiling water to melt and spread.

    Fine powders to include:

    • 1 ounce each of:
      • Ai Wei (Ferula)
      • Ding Xiang (Clove)
      • Chen Xiang (Agarwood)
    • 2 ounces of:
      • She Xiang (Musk)
      • Xue Jie (Dragon's Blood)
      • Hai Er Cha (Child's Tea)
      • Ru Xiang (Frankincense)
      • Mo Yao (Myrrh) — each 3 ounces
    • 5 qian (15 grams) of pearl powder,
    • 3 qian (9 grams) of amber.

    Grind these into extremely fine powder, and incorporate into the previous ointment.[63p]

    Ginseng and Astragalus Decoction: Treats conditions associated with leukorrhea due to deficiency of both qi and blood, as well as continuous bleeding. Adjust as needed. Ingredients: Ginseng, pan-fried Astragalus, Dong Quai, pan-fried Atractylodes, pan-fried White Peony, mugwort leaves, each 3 grams; prepared donkey-hide gelatin, 6 grams. Prepare two doses, decoct in water and take.

    Six-Flavor Pill, also known as Rehmannia Pill: Treats leukorrhea along with deficiencies in the kidney leading to heat symptoms such as thirst, sputum, and frequent, painful urination. Symptoms include dizziness, dry throat, cracked lips, loose teeth, and soreness in the lower back and legs. Use this formula combined as needed. Ingredients: Cooked Rehmannia 480 grams, Cornelian Cherry, Chinese Yam each 240 grams, White Poria, Alisma, and Moutan Bark each 180 grams. Process into pills the size of a walnut and take before meals.

    Modified Xiao Yao Powder: Treats leukorrhea with heat in the liver; adjust as needed. Ingredients: Honey-fried Licorice, stir-fried Dong Quai, stir-fried Peony with wine, Poria, pan-fried Atractylodes, Chai Hu each 3 grams; Moutan Bark and stir-fried Gardenia each 2.5 grams. Prepare by decocting in water and take.

    Bu Gong Pill (Wang's formula, same as below): Treats leukorrhea due to deficiency and prolapse of the lower jiao; strengthens the condition. Ingredients: Deer Horn Powder, White Poria, Atractylodes, White Peony, White Angelica, calcined Dragon Bone, calcined Oysters, stir-fried Chinese Yam, calcined Red Stone Fat, all in equal parts; pan-fried Ginger, in half quantity. Form into pills soaked in vinegar and take with empty stomach rice drink.[65p]

    　　震灵丹　一名紫金舟。治妇人血气不足，崩漏虚损，带下虚冷，胎脏无子。　　滴乳香另研　五灵脂　没药并去砂石，各二两　朱砂飞一两　禹余粮火煅酢淬手捻得碎为度　紫石英　代赭石如禹余粮炮制　赤石脂以上四味，并作小块，入锅内盐泥固济候干，用炭十斤，煅通红，火尽为度，入地埋，出火毒二宿　　右为细末，以糯米粉煮糊为丸如鸡头实大，晒干出火，每一丸，空心酢汤下。如有孕，不可服。[66p]

    San Bu Wan: For treating red discharge, take this pill.
    Ingredients: Huang Qin, Huang Lian, Huang Yao, each stir-fried in equal parts, mixed with honey to form pills, taken with warm water.

    Si Wu Jia Qin Lian Tang: For those with excessive heat and discharge.
    Ingredients: Si Wu Decoction, Chi Shao, Huang Qin stir-fried, Huang Lian stir-fried, each one qian; Gan Cao Sheng five fen. Decoct and take with water.

    Jia Wei Liu Jun Zi Tang: For treating white discharge.
    Ingredients: Chen Pi, Ban Xia prepared, Cang Zhu soaked with water, Ren Shen each one qian; Bai Zhu one qian five fen; Bai Fu one qian two fen; Zhi Cao seven fen; Sheng Ma, Chai Hu each five fen. Decoct with ginger water and take.

    Zhen Ling Dan, also known as Zi Jin Zhou: Treats women with insufficient blood and qi, uterine bleeding, cold discharge, and infertility.
    Ingredients: Ding Ru Xiang ground separately, Wu Ling Zhi, Mo Yao without sand and stones, each two liang; Zhu Sha one liang; Yu Yu Liang roasted, crushed to measure; Zi Shi Ying, Dai Zhe Shi prepared the same way as Yu Yu Liang; Chi Shi Zhi and the above four flavors made into small pieces, placed in a pot with salt mud, dried; use ten jin of charcoal, calcine until red hot, then covered and buried, to eliminate toxicity for two nights.
    Grind into fine powder, mix with glutinous rice flour to make pills the size of a chicken egg, sun-dry, and take with vinegar soup. Do not take if pregnant.[66p]

    Gu Chang Pill
    For treating dampness leading to diarrhea, blood in stool, and white discharge, to be used after expelling spleen and stomach accumulation, to dry out dampness. Often used in combination with decoctions.
    Ingredients: Chuanren.[68p]

    　　右为末，粥糊为丸服。按此药，性凉而燥，须炒用。一方加滑石一半。　　又方　治白带因七情所伤脉数者。
    　　黄连炒　侧柏叶酒蒸　黄蘗炒，各半两　白芍　香附子酢炒　白朮炒，各一两　白芷烧存性　木香各三钱　椿根皮二两，炒　　右为末，饭粥为丸，米饮汤送下。已上五方，治带俱用。椿皮，乃凉燥之剂，湿热盛者宜之。后一方有黄连、香附、木香，故可治七情所伤。
    　　乳香散　治赤白带下。
    　　草果一枚去皮，入乳香一小块，用面饼裹，火炮焦黄留性，取出和面用之　　右为细末，每服二钱，陈皮饮调下，重者三钱。
    　　伏龙肝散　治赤白带下，久患不瘥，尩悴乏力，人脉微濡。　　伏龙肝炒令烟尽　屋梁上悬尘炒令烟尽　棕榈烧赤存性　　右，并出火毒，等分研匀，入脑麝各少许，每服三钱，温酒或淡酢汤下。患十年者，半月可愈。[69p]

    The first part is a prescription where the powder is made into pills with congee. This medicine is cool and drying in nature, so it should be fried before use. One variation adds half a portion of talc.

    Another formula treats white discharge caused by emotional distress, with a rapid pulse. The ingredients are: half a tael each of fried Huanglian, steamed Cèbǎi leaves with wine, and fried Huangbo; one tael each of Bai Shao, vinegar-fried Xiangfuzi, and fried Baizhu; three qian each of burnt Baizhi and Mu Xiang; two taels of fried Chun gen pi. This is all ground into a powder, made into pills with congee, and taken with rice soup. The previous five formulas can treat various types of discharge. The Chun pi is a cool and drying agent, suitable for cases of excess damp heat. The last formula contains Huanglian, Xiangfu, and Mu Xiang, so it can treat issues caused by emotional distress.

    The Ruxiang powder treats both red and white discharge. One grass fruit, peeled, combined with a small piece of Ruxiang, is wrapped in a dough cake and roasted until golden brown. This mixture is then ground into a fine powder, and the dosage is two qian per serving, mixed with dried tangerine peel infusion for consumption, with three qian for more severe cases.

    The Fulonggansan treats red and white discharge that has persisted for a long time without improvement, associated with fatigue and a weak pulse. Fulonggan is fried until the smoke dissipates, dust from the roof beams is fried until smoke clears, and palm fronds are burned to retain their essence. These are all equally divided and finely ground, then small amounts of musk are added. The dosage is three qian, taken with warm wine or diluted vinegar soup. In cases lasting ten years, it can lead to recovery in half a month.[69p]

    Mǎtíwán - Treats continuous leucorrhea.
    White horse hoof, Yuyu grain each four taels, dragon bone three taels, white silkworm, fish bones, red stone resin each two taels; grind into fine powder, refine with honey and form into pills the size of a wutong seed. Take ten pills, wash down with empty stomach wine; do not exceed thirty pills.

    Báizhǐsǎn - Treats red and white leucorrhea.
    Two taels of white peony, two pieces of dried cuttlefish, one piece of calcined fetal hair; grind into fine powder, take two qian mixed with warm wine on an empty stomach.

    Mǔlìsǎn - Treats excessive leucorrhea and menstruation, or sudden blood loss, regardless of duration.
    Oyster, dragon bone, red stone resin both calcined, rejuvenated meat, cut and baked, dendrobium, fish bones without shells, astragalus each half tael; cow horn (horn thought) ash, stir-fried ejiao, roasted cooked rehmannia, stir-fried peony each two taels; dried ginger, ginseng, white atractylodes, mulberry ear, roasted angelica each one tael and two and a half qian; cyathula, fried aconite peeled and female navel, cinnamon heart, stir-fried mugwort each one tael. Grind thoroughly into fine powder, take three qian, mixed with rice drink at dawn, twice daily.

    Bǔgōngwán (Dān xī) - Treats white discharge and excessive libido.
    Deer antler powder, white poria, white peony, white atractylodes, fish bones, self-peony, oyster powder, white bellflower, yam each in equal parts; grind to powder, mix into balls the size of wutong seeds, take fifty pills washed down with rice drink.[70p]

    White Alum Pill
    Used to treat women's red and white vaginal discharge that is chronic and has not healed, resulting in thin, sallow skin, and continuous menstrual bleeding for years with no effect from other medicines. The pulse is soft and weak. When taken with the previous Fu Long Gan San, it can lead to recovery.
    Ingredients:

    • Four ounces of white alum
    • Two ounces of aconite
    • Four ounces of yellow dog head bone, charred to ash

    Grind the above into a fine powder, form into pills the size of tungs, and take thirty pills each time.

    Bu Zhen Run Chang Decoction (also known as Assist Yang Decoction)
    Used to treat white vaginal discharge, pain in the vulva, urgent pain in the heart area, a sallow complexion, loose skin, a heavy body, and a feeling of ice in the genitals.
    Ingredients:

    • 1.2 grams of bupleurum
    • 2 grams of ginger
    • Seven flowers of white chrysanthemum
    • 1 gram of saposhnikovia
    • 1 gram of jujube kernel
    • 1 gram of dried ginger
    • 1 gram of licorice
    • 0.5 grams of dried tangerine peel
    • 0.5 grams of fresh honeysuckle

    Grind these ingredients into a fine powder, using for one dose, boil in two cups of water until reduced to one cup, strain, and take hot before meals. The slippery properties of chrysanthemum and jujube kernel are beneficial for dryness and blockage.

    Preparation for Treating Vaginal Discharge

    1. Grind turtle shell with wine and roast 2 taels of rhubarb and 1 tael of dried ginger. Add 1 qian of dried bitter orange. Mix together into a powder, form into pills with wine, to be taken twice daily, 70 pills each time.

    2. Another formula for treating frequent vaginal discharge:

      • 1 jin of goji root
      • 5 taels of raw rehmannia
        Boil these two ingredients in 10 dou (a volume measurement) of water to extract 5 sheng. Divide into three doses.

    The above three formulas treat vaginal discharge using turtle shell, rhubarb, and rehmannia, suitable for those with deficiency of true kidney yin.

    White Lans Formula (from the "Jisheng Fang"):
    For treating young women with cold deficiency in the Chong and Ren channels, resulting in pure white vaginal discharge:

    • 2 taels of deer antler, steamed and roasted
    • 1 tael of white land, and 1 tael of dog spine prepared by burning off hair
      Grind these into a fine powder, mix with mugwort and vinegar juice, mold into pills the size of a walnut, taking 50 pills each time with warm wine on an empty stomach.

    • 1 tael of white peony
    • 1 tael of prepared donkey-hide gelatin

    • 1 tael of Chinese teasel soaked in wine
      And ½ tael of asarum. Grind these into a powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of a walnut. Take 50 pills on an empty stomach with rice congee.[72p]

    　　茯苓散　治妇人血伤兼带下，积久不止，面黄体瘦，渐成虚劳，腰脚沉重，胎气多损。　　白茯苓　菖蒲　木香　熟地黄焙　诃黎勒皮　柏子仁研　杜仲炙　青橘皮去白焙　赤石脂　鰞鲗鱼骨去甲　五加皮銼　艾叶烧灰　秦艽　牛角(角思)灰　兔丝子酒浸另捣　当归焙，各一两　　右为细末，每服二钱，温酒调下，糯米饮亦得。如有胎息，用鲤鱼糯米粥下药。
    　　卷柏丸　治妇人室女腹脏冷热相攻，心腹绞痛，腰腿疼，赤白带下，面色痿黄，四肢羸乏。　　卷柏酢炙　鹿茸酢炙　桑寄生　艾叶酢炒　白石脂　赤石脂　代赭石各火煅，酢淬七次　当归酒浸炒　芎藭　鳖甲酢炙　地榆各一两　木香不见火　龙骨各半两　干姜炮，七钱半　黄芪蜜炙　熟地黄洗，各一两半　　右为细末，酢煮糯米丸和丸如梧桐子大，每服七十丸，空心米饮送下。[73p]

    Fuling San: This formula treats women with blood injuries combined with leukorrhea, persistent for a long time. Symptoms include a yellowish face, emaciation, gradual onset of deficiency labor, heaviness in the waist and legs, and significant damage to fetal energy.

    Ingredients: White Fuling, Acorus, Mu Xiang, roasted Shudi, Acalypha, ground Bai Zi Ren, roasted Du Zhong, white part of Qing Ju Pi, red stone resin, fish bone of the fence lizard (skinned), shavings of Wu Jia Pi, burned Ai Ye, Qin Jiao, ash from ox horn (horn thinking), rabbit silk soaked in wine and then ground, roasted Dang Gui; each ingredient is one tael.

    These should be ground into a fine powder. Take two qian with warm wine or glutinous rice drink. If there are fetal movements, use carp and glutinous rice porridge to take the medicine.

    Juanbai Wan: This formula treats women with abdominal organs attacked by cold and heat, causing severe abdominal pain, lower back and leg pain, red and white leukorrhea, pale yellow complexion, and weak limbs.

    Ingredients: Vine of Juanbai (vine-grain), deer antler, mulberry mistletoe, Ai Ye sautéed in vinegar, white stone resin, red stone resin, and Dai Zhe Shi all fire calcined and treated with vinegar seven times; Dang Gui soaked in wine then sautéed, Chuan Xiong, turtle shell treated with vinegar, and Di Yu, each one tael; Xiang Mu (Mu Xiang does not see fire) and Long Gu, half a tael each; Gan Jiang processed, seven qian and half; Huang Qi honey-roasted; and Shudi washed, each one and a half tael.

    These should also be ground into a fine powder, cooked with vinegar, and made into glutinous rice pills the size of wutong seeds. Take seventy pills on an empty stomach, accompanied by rice drink.[73p]

    　　艾煎丸　治妇人一切虚寒，胎前产后，赤白带下，或成血瘕，久服此药，自然融化。　　伏道艾叶去尘土枝梗，先用大枣肉十二两煮烂，同艾叶捶烂如泥，捻作薄饼，猛火焙干，急碾为末　汉椒去目枝梗及合口者秤，各五两，以阿胶二两、米酢三升，同椒于砂瓶内煮极干，取出焙干燥为末　当归酒浸　川芎　白薇　附子大者炮去皮脐　白芍药　卷柏取青叶　泽兰叶去枝梗各焙干　熟地黄净洗漉去浮者，晒干酒浸蒸晒，再入酒浸蒸五七次，如糖煎香美方可用。亦焙干秤，各三两　　右同为细末，与前艾末椒末拌匀，米酢煮糊和丸如梧桐子大，每服五七十丸至百丸二百丸，空心艾酢汤送下。[74p]

    Ai Jian Wan treats all instances of deficiency and cold in women, before and after childbirth, includes conditions like red or white discharge, or blood masses. Long-term use of this medicine will naturally dissolve these issues.

    Prepare by cleaning mugwort leaves of dirt and stems, then cook twelve taels of jujube flesh until soft. Mash together with the mugwort leaves into a paste, form thin cakes, and bake quickly over a strong fire until dry, then grind into a fine powder.

    Remove the stems and seed heads from five taels each of Sichuan pepper and other spices; in a sand bottle, boil with two taels of donkey-hide gelatin and three sheng of rice vinegar until completely dry, then take out and dry again into a powder.

    Soak Dong quai, Chuanxiong, Baiwei, and large Aconite (remove skin and navel) in wine; dry and mash them well. Clean and wash cooked Rehmannia, drying it after soaking in wine and steaming it several times until fragrant and syrupy, then dry again, measuring three taels of each.

    Combine all these powders evenly together with the previously prepared mugwort and pepper powders, mix with rice vinegar to make a dough, and form pills the size of wutong seeds. Take five to seventy pills at a time, up to two hundred, to be swallowed with mugwort vinegar soup on an empty stomach.[74p]

    　　沉香牡丹丸　治妇人血海久虚，经候不利，赤白带下，血气冲心，多发刺痛，四肢烦困。　　沉香七钱半　牡丹皮　赤芍药　当归　巴戟　吴茱萸汤泡去苦炒　桂心　黄芪蜜炙　川芎　人参　茯苓　山药　橘红　干生姜　白龙骨　木香　白朮　牛膝酒洗　枳壳麸炒　肉豆蔻　厚朴制，各半两　　右为细末，炼蜜和丸如梧桐子大，每服二十丸，空心温酒下。若心腹痛，白芷煎酒下。[75p]

    Chénxiāng Mǔdān Wán
    This formula treats women suffering from prolonged blood deficiency, painful menstruation, unusual discharge of red and white, and a surging of blood and qi causing stabbing pains and heaviness in the limbs.

    Ingredients:

    • 7.5 qian of sandalwood
    • Peony root
    • Red peony root
    • Angelica sinensis
    • Morinda root
    • Wu zhu yu (dried) simmered to remove bitterness and stir-fried
    • Cinnamon heart
    • Honey-fried astragalus
    • Chuan xiong (Ligusticum)
    • Ginseng
    • Poria
    • Yam
    • Tangerine peel
    • Dried ginger
    • White dragon bone
    • Wood fragrance
    • White atractylodes
    • Chinese angelica, washed with wine
    • Bitter orange peel stir-fried
    • Nutmeg
    • Magnolia bark, each ingredient in equal parts of 2 liang.

    Grind the above into a fine powder, then mix with honey to form pills about the size of walnuts. Take 20 pills with warm wine on an empty stomach. If there are abdominal pains, take white atractylodes boiled in wine.[75p]

    　　紫桂丸　补益血海，治冲任气虚，经脉不调，腰痛腹痛，冷带崩漏。　　禹余粮火煅酢淬七次，三两　龙骨　艾叶酢炒　赤石脂　牡蛎煅　地榆各二两　厚朴　当归　牡丹皮　阿胶蛤粉炒成珠子吴茱萸汤洗　香白芷　肉桂去粗皮，各一两　附子炮，半两　　右为末，面糊为丸梧桐子大，每服三十丸，浓煎酢汤下。
    　　固真丸　治白带久下不止，脐腹冷痛，其寒扪之如冰，阴中亦然，目中溜火上壅，视物(目巟)(目巟)无所见，齿皆恶热，饮即痛，须得黄连末擦之，其痛乃止。惟喜干食，大恶汤饮。　　白石脂烧赤水飞研细晒干　柴胡各一钱　白龙骨酒煮水飞晒干，二钱　当归酒洗，三钱　干姜炮，四钱　黄蘗酒洗　白芍各五分　　右为细末，水煮稀糊为丸如鸡头大，每服三十丸，空心宿食消尽，煎百沸汤放温送下。无令胃中停住，待少时，以早膳压之，是不令热药犯胃。忌生冷硬物与酒湿面。按石脂、龙骨之濇以去脱也，盖湿多滑脱者宜之。[76p]

    Ziguim Pill: Nourishes the blood sea, treats deficiency of the Chong and Ren channels, regulates the meridians, alleviates lower back pain and abdominal pain, and addresses cold discharges and irregular bleeding. Prepare by calcining Yu Yu Liang and vinegar seven times, three taels; Dragon Bone, Ai Ye (mugwort), each two taels; red stone resin, oyster shell, and Di Yu (ground rhubarb) each two taels; Hou Po (magnolia bark), Dang Gui (Angelica), Mu Dan Pi (peony root), and Ejiao (donkey-hide gelatin) with fried ha powder made into beads; wash in Wu Zhu Yu decoction. Also include Xiang Bai Zhi (white angelica) and Rou Gui (cinnamon) after removing the coarse skin, each one tael; Fu Zi (aconite) processed, half a tael. Grind into a powder, form into pills the size of a wutong seed, and take thirty pills each time with a concentrated vinegar decoction.

    Guo Zhen Pill: Treats prolonged and unceasing white discharge, cold pain in the navel and abdomen, where touching feels like ice, also affecting the yin. There is fire rising in the eyes causing vision problems (things appearing blurry), teeth feel hot, and drinking causes pain; need to apply powdered Huang Lian to relieve the pain. Prefer dry foods and greatly avoid soup and drinks. Prepare by burning white stone resin in red water, grinding finely, and drying; Chai Hu (bupleurum) each one qian; white dragon bone boiled in wine, dried and ground, two qian; wash Dang Gui in wine, three qian; dry ginger processed, four qian; Huang Bo (golden thread) washed in wine; Bai Shao (white peony) each five fen. Grind into a fine powder, form into pills the size of a chicken's head, take thirty pills on an empty stomach to eliminate food stagnation, and send down with warm decoction boiled three times. Don't let it stagnate in the stomach; wait a while and suppress it with breakfast so as not to let hot medicine offend the stomach. Avoid raw, cold, hard foods and alcoholic wet foods. The properties of stone resin and dragon bone help with mucus detachment, thus suitable for those with excess dampness.[76p]

    　　茅花散　治妇人血崩不止，赤白带下。　　茅花一握　棕榈树皮三寸　嫩荷叶三张　甘草节二寸　　右为细末，空心，酒调半匙服。

    　　苦楝丸　治妇人赤白带。
    　　苦楝碎酒浸　茴香炒　当归各等分
    　　右为末，酒糊丸，每服三五十丸，空心温酒下。如腰腿疼，四物汤四两，加羌活、防风各一两，煎汤送下。
    　　地榆膏　治赤白带下骨立者。
    　　地榆一斤
    　　右用水三升，煎至一半，去滓再煎如稠钖，绞净，空心服三合，日二服。一方用地榆三两，酢水煎服。按治带用地榆，寒濇之剂也，亦湿热盛而滑脱者宜之。又方书云：地榆本血分之药，而其性寒，故凡血分有热而妄行者，能止之，非濇剂也。
    　　豆花散　治妇人白崩。
    　　白扁豆花焙干
    　　右为末，炒米煮饮，入烧盐，空心服，数次即效。紫花勿用。[77p]

    Mao Hua San: Used to treat women's continuous uterine bleeding and red and white discharges.

    • Mao Hua (cattail flower) one handful
    • Palm bark three inches
    • Tender lotus leaves three
    • Licorice root two inches
      All ingredients should be ground into fine powder, mixed with a hollowed-out space, and taken with half a spoonful of wine.

    Ku Lin Wan: Used to treat red and white discharges in women.

    • Ku Lin (melia) crushed and soaked in wine
    • Fennel roasted
    • Angelica, in equal parts
      All ingredients should be ground into powder, made into pills with wine, and taken 30 to 50 pills on an empty stomach with warm wine. If there is pain in the waist and legs, prepare Si Wu Tang (Four Substance Decoction) four taels, adding one tael each of Qiang Huo (Notopterygium) and Fang Feng (Siler), and decoct the soup to take.

    Di Yu Gao: Used to treat severe red and white discharges that cause bone pain.

    • Di Yu (Japanese knotweed) one jin
      Use three sheng (liters) of water, boil until reduced by half, strain and reboil until thick, then filter. Take three he (120 ml) on an empty stomach, two times a day. An alternative method uses three liang (150 grams) of Di Yu boiled in vinegar water for consumption. It is noted that Di Yu is used for treating discharges and is a chilly, damp remedy suitable for conditions of excess heat that are slippery and draining. Additionally, some texts state that Di Yu is primarily a blood remedy, characterized by its cold nature; thus, it can stop errant heat in blood conditions, making it not merely a slippery remedy.

    Dou Hua San: Used to treat women's white bleeding.

    • White hyacinth bean flowers, dried
      Grind into powder, mix with roasted rice for a drink, add burned salt, and take on an empty stomach for effective results in a short time. Avoid using purple flowers.[77p]

    　　调经补真汤　冬后一月，微有地泥冰泮，其白带再来，阴户中寒，一服立止，大进饮食。　　麻黄五分，不去节　人参　白朮　当归　黄芩　升麻根　甘草炙，各五分　杏仁三枚　泽泻　良姜各一钱　黄芪七分　桂枝少许　干姜炮　苍朮各二分　柴胡　羌活各四分　防风　独活　槁本各二分　白葵花七朵，去萼　　右除黄芩、麻黄外，都为粗末，先将水二盏，煎麻黄一味，令沸，掠去沫，入余药，同煎至二盏，再入生黄芩煎至一盏，去滓稍热服，空心宿食消尽，日高服之。一时许，可食早膳。
    　　本事地黄丸 【《准绳》，下同】 　治妇人月经不调，每行数日不止，兼有白带，渐渐瘦悴，饮食少味，累年无子。　　熟地黄二两　山茱萸　白芜荑　白芍药微炒　干姜　代赭石火煅酢淬，各一两　厚朴姜炙　白僵蚕各半两　　右细末，炼蜜丸桐子大，每服四五十丸，空心酒下，日三服。此庞老方也。[78p]

    Regulating Menstruation and Nourishing Essence Decoction

    One month after winter, when there is slight thawing and moist earth, if there is a recurrence of white discharge and coldness in the genitals, one dose will promptly stop it, allowing for increased eating and drinking.

    • Ephedra: 5 fen, without removing the nodes
    • Ginseng: 5 fen
    • Atractylodes: 5 fen
    • Angelica: 5 fen
    • Scutellaria: 5 fen
    • Bupleurum root: 5 fen
    • Licorice (roasted): 5 fen
    • Apricot kernels: 3 pieces
    • Alisma: 1 qian
    • Zingiberzerumbet: 1 qian
    • Astragalus: 7 fen
    • Cinnamon twig: a little
    • Dried ginger (prepared): 2 fen
    • Atractylodes: 2 fen
    • Bupleurum: 4 fen
    • Saposhnikovia: 2 fen
    • Angelica Pubescens: 2 fen
    • White hibiscus flowers: 7 flowers (sepals removed)

    Excluding Scutellaria and Ephedra, all should be ground into coarse powder. First, take two bowls of water to decoct the Ephedra alone until boiling, skim off the foam, then add the remaining herbs and decoct until there is two bowls left. Next, add fresh Scutellaria and decoct until there is one bowl. Strain the dregs and take it warm on an empty stomach after digestion; consume this when the sun is high. After some time, one can eat an early breakfast.

    Basic Earth Yellow Pill

    This treats women with irregular menstruation, where it lasts several days without stopping, accompanied by white discharge, gradual weight loss, diminished appetite, and years without pregnancy.

    • Cooked Rehmannia: 2 liang
    • Cornelian Cherry: 1 liang
    • White Erigeron: 1 liang
    • White Peony (slightly stir-fried): 1 liang
    • Dried Ginger: 1 liang
    • Substituted Calamine Stone: 1 liang (calcined)
    • Magnolia (roasted): 0.5 liang
    • Silkworms: 0.5 liang

    Grind these into fine powder, mix with honey to form pill-sized pieces of tung oil, taking 40 to 50 pills each time, swallowed with alcohol on an empty stomach, three times a day. This is the formula from the revered elder Pang.[78p]

    Gui Fu Decoction treats foul-smelling leucorrhea, excessive sorrow and unhappiness, and severe coldness. The ingredients are: 1 qian of cinnamon, 3 qian of chuanwu, and 5 fen each of berberine and anemarrhena. Grind these into a coarse powder, prepare one dose with 2 cups of water, and boil down to 1 cup. Take it warm after meals. If feeling constantly full despite eating little, add 5 fen of white peony. If there is loss of appetite, add 20 pieces of five-flavor fruit. If there are feelings of distress and numbness on the face as if insects are crawling, indicating extreme deficiency of the stomach's vital energy, add 1 qian of astragalus, 7 fen of ginseng, 2 fen of licorice, and 5 fen of ramie.

    Xiang Fu Liu He Decoction treats both red and white discharge.

    Four Substance Decoction includes: fennel, cinnamon, and cyperus. Combine and simmer for use.

    Another formula treats red and white discharge that has persisted for a long time. It contains 2 taels of white peony and 0.5 taels of dried ginger. Fry each until yellow and grind into powder. Take 2 qian with empty stomach rice drink, two times daily.

    Er Dou San treats ear ringing, heart agitation, heaviness in the waist and legs, internal emptiness with rumbling in the abdomen, coldness below the navel, and frequent watery discharge resembling muddy fluid. The ingredients are: 1 tael each of white cardamom, nutmeg, clove, poria, morinda root, cinnamon bark, and black aconite, and 0.5 tael each of ginseng, white atractylodes, chinese yam, balloon flower, fennel, and powder grass. Crush into pieces and take 3 qian each time, with 1.5 cups of water, 3 slices of ginger, and 3 leaves of perilla. Boil down to 70% remaining, strain, and take warm on an empty stomach.[79p]

    　　鹤顶丸　治室女经水初下，或浴冷水，或热而扇，或当风，及妇人阴阳过多，血水相连而下，并产后带下。　　当归七钱半，酒浸　附子半两，炮去皮　干姜炮　龙骨盐泥煅吴茱萸汤泡　赤石脂火煅酢淬，各一两半　牡蛎一两三钱，盐泥煅艾叶一两，酢煮　　右为细末研匀，酢糊和丸如梧子大，以赤石脂末为衣，每服五十丸，空心，用艾叶盐汤或乌梅煎汤下。

    Heron Top Pill
    Treats the initial menstrual flow of young women, whether due to bathing in cold water, fanning after warming, or exposure to wind, as well as excessive yin and yang in women, leading to blood and water flowing down together, and postnatal discharge.

    Nourishing Qi and Activating Blood Pill

    Treats labor injuries affecting the Chong and Ren meridians, and conditions of red and white discharge.

    Ingredients:

    • Charred Da Ai Ye (Mugwort) 5 taels
    • Dried Ginger, ground 2.5 taels
    • Fu Zi (Aconite)
    • Bai Shao Yao (White Peony)
    • Bai Zhu (Atractylodes)
    • Ju Hong (Tangerine Peel)
    • Chuan Xiong (Ligusticum Chuanxiong)
    • Dang Gui (Angelica Sinensis)
    • Ren Shen (Ginseng)
    • Ba Ji Tian (Morinda Root) (remove heart)
    • Roasted Glutinous Rice
    • Wu Wei Zi (Schisandra) 2 taels each

    Preparation:
    Take the dried ginger and mugwort, use 2 liters of vinegar, 2 liters of non-ash liquor, and 2 liters of fresh ginger juice. Place the dried ginger and mugwort in a silver container, simmer with low heat until it forms a paste. Grind the Fu Zi and the other nine ingredients into fine powder, add to the paste and warm. Mix with 2.5 taels of cooked wheat flour to form a dough. Roll into pills about the size of a jujube, taking 50 pills with warm wine or rice drink.

    Zhuyur Bath Decoction

    Treats cold and deficiency in the lower region, abdominal pain around the navel, multi-colored discharge, irregular menstruation or bleeding, and stagnant urination.

    Ingredients:

    • Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia) decoction
    • Du Zhong (Eucommia Bark), roasted to remove fibers
    • She Chuang Zi (Cynomorium)
    • Wu Wei Zi (Schisandra)
    • Ding Pi (Cortex Citri) 1 tael each
    • Mu Xiang (Aucklandia)
    • Ding Xiang (Clove) half tael each

    Preparation:
    Shred the ingredients to the size of soybeans. Use half a tael in a silk bag, boil in 3 large bowls of water until it simmers. While hot, apply the steam to the lower body, using hands for steam bathing, morning and evening twice.[81p]

    　　坐药龙盐骨　治同上。

    　　酒煮当归丸　治癫癎，白带下疰，脚气，腰已下如在冰雪中，以火焙炕，重厚绵衣盖上，犹冷不任，面白如枯鱼，肌如刀削，小便不止，与白带长流而不禁固，自不知觉，目青蓝如菜色，(目巟)(目巟)无所见，身重如山，行步敧侧，不能安地，腿膝枯细，大便秘结，口不能言，无力之极，食不下，心下痞烦，心懊憹，面停垢，背恶寒，哕呕不止，脉沉厥紧而濇，按之空虚。　　当归一两　黑附子炮去皮脐　良姜各七钱　炒黄盐　茴香　丁香各半两　延胡索四钱　全蝎三钱　柴胡　升麻根　木香各二钱　苦楝子　甘草炙，各五分　　右将当归、茴香、附子、良姜四味，銼如麻豆大，以好酒一升，同煮至酒尽为度，炭火焙干，同为极细末；又将炒黄盐以下九味细末之，共合一处拌匀，酒煮面糊为丸如桐子大，每服二十丸，空心宿食消尽，淡酢汤下。忌油腻冷物酒面。[83p]

    Alcohol-infused Angelica Pills treat epilepsy, excessive vaginal discharge, beriberi, and a feeling of coldness in the lower back as if one were in ice and snow. Even when warmed by fire and covered with heavy woolen clothing, one still feels cold; the face becomes pale like a dried fish, the skin is thin as if shaved with a knife, and urination is unending, accompanied by continuous vaginal discharge without awareness. The eyes are blue like vegetable color, with obscured vision, the body feels as heavy as a mountain, walking is unsteady, unable to find a stable position. The legs and knees are thin and withered, there is constipation, speech is impossible, extreme weakness persists, appetite is lost, there is a feeling of fullness and discomfort in the heart, and the face appears dull. The back feels cold, there are continuous belching and vomiting; the pulse is deep, tight, and weak, with a hollow feeling upon palpation.

    Ingredients:
    1 tael of angelica,
    7 qian each of black aconite (peeled), and ginger,
    half a tael each of fennel and clove,
    4 qian of Corydalis,
    3 qian of whole scorpion,
    2 qian each of Bupleurum, Cimicifuga root, and costus,
    5 fen each of bitter neem seed and honey-fried licorice.

    Preparation: Take the four ingredients (angelica, fennel, aconite, ginger) and grind them to the size of mung beans. Simmer in one sheng of good wine until the wine reduces completely. Dry them over charcoal, then grind to a very fine powder. Combine with the remaining nine finely ground ingredients, mix thoroughly, and form a paste with wine to create pills the size of jujubes. Take twenty pills on an empty stomach with dilute vinegar soup. Avoid greasy or cold substances and wine.[83p]

It can also be ground into powder, water-floated, and taken daily in amounts from half a cash to one cash, mixed with rice drink, until all ailments are resolved in a month.

    For women’s white discharge, often caused by emotional stress or coldness in the lower body: Use sand ginseng powdered, taking two cash per dose mixed in rice drink.

    For women’s multicolored discharge: Make seven pancakes using flour, place them on red-hot yellow ancient bricks, cover with yellow (plantain) leaves, and put two layers of cloth over them. Have the patient sit on top so that the medicinal vapor enters the abdomen, which should result in worms exiting like silkworms, healing in no more than three to five treatments.

    For white discharge with burning sensation: Mix equal parts of white cock’s comb flower and bitter gourd, burn to preserve properties, and take with empty fire wine.

    For women’s white discharge: Take four ounces of white angelica, half a pound of slaked lime, soak for three nights, then grind and fry it into powder. Take two cash with wine, twice daily.

    For red and white vaginal discharge with absent menstruation: Use equal parts of snake bed seed and dried white alum, grind into powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of a marble, coat with rouge, and insert into the vagina; change when warm, once daily.[90p]

    　　赤白带下：苦参二两、牡蛎粉一两五钱为末，以雄猪肚一个，水三碗，煮烂捣泥，和丸梧子大，每服百丸，温酒下。【积德堂】
    　　赤白带下，年深诸药不能疗者：用贯众状如刺猬者一个，全用不銼，只揉去毛及花萼，以好酢蘸湿，慢火炙令香熟，候冷为末，米饮空心每服二钱，甚效。【《妇人良方》】
    　　白带白淫：风化石灰一两，白茯苓三两为末，糊丸梧子大，每服二三十丸，空心米饮下。【集元方】
    　　赤白带下，夏枯草花开时采，阴干为求，每服二钱，米饮下，食前服。 【《家传方》】
    　　妇人白带：白鸡冠花晒干为末，每旦空心酒服三钱。赤带用红者。 【《集效方》】
    　　下血血崩，或五色漏带：香附子去毛，炒焦为末，极热，酒服二钱，立愈。昏迷甚者三钱，米饮下。亦可加椶灰。【《本事方》】
    　　赤白带下，及血崩不止者：香附子、赤芍药等分为末，盐一捻，水二盏，煎一盏，食前温服。【《圣惠》，下同】[91p]

    1. For red and white vaginal discharge: Two taels of Baicalensis, one and a half taels of oyster powder, ground to a fine powder; take one male pig's stomach, add three bowls of water, boil until soft, mash into a paste, and form into small pills the size of a walnut. Take one hundred pills with warm wine.

    　　妇人带下，脐腹冷痛，面色痿黄，日渐虚困：用葵花一两，阴干为末，每空心温酒服二钱匕。赤带用赤葵，白带用白葵。

    For red and white discharge: fry buckwheat until charred, grind it into powder, and make into pills the size of wutong nuts. Take fifty pills with salty soup three times a day.

    　　　　针灸

    　　《甲乙经》曰：妇人乳子下赤白，腰俞主之。　　妇人下赤白，沃后，阴中干痛，恶合阴阳，少腹(月真)坚，小便闭，曲骨主之。【一本作屈骨。】　　妇人下赤白，里急瘈瘲，五枢主之。　　女子下苍汁，不禁赤沥，阴中痒痛，少腹控(月少)，不可俯仰，下髎主之。刺腰尻交者，两胂上，以月死生为痏数，发针立已。　　女子疝瘕，按之如以汤沃两股中，少腹肿，阴挺出痛，阴水来下，阴中肿或痒，漉青汁若葵羹，血闭无子，不嗜食，曲泉主之。　　《千金方》曰：月事不利，见赤白而有身反败阴寒，刺行间入六分，灸三壮。穴在足大趾间动脉应手。　　赤白里急瘈瘲，刺五枢入一寸，灸五壮，穴在带脉下三寸。[94p]

    Red and white vaginal discharge: Take one slice of pig liver and roast it with powdered haritaki, roasting repeatedly until half a tael of powder is used. Chew finely on an empty stomach and wash it down with aged rice wine.

    For women's white discharge: Fry the seeds of winter melon into a powder and take five qian with rice wine on an empty stomach.

    Acupuncture and Moxibustion:

    The "Jia Yi Jing" states: For women with red and white discharge, treat at the waist (yao) and below. When women experience red and white discharge with dryness and pain in the genitals and a firm lower abdomen, with difficulty urinating, treat at the pubic bone. In cases of red and white discharge with urgent abdominal pain, treat at the five pivots. For women with dark green discharge, if there is unmanageable red dripping, itching and pain in the genitals, and a tendency to stoop, treat at the lower back.

    For female hernias, if the abdomen is swollen, and there is pain when the genital area protrudes, with discharge and swelling or itching, use blue juice like a soup; in cases of blood blockage with no appetite, treat at the crux of the foot.

    The "Qian Jin Fang" states: If menstruation is obstructed and there is red and white with possible conception, treat with thick needles in the interstitial spaces, and use three moxibustion treatments. The point is located in the artery between the big toe and the hand.

    For red and white discharge with abdominal urgency, needle the five pivots one inch deep and apply five moxibustion treatments. The point is three inches below the belt vessel.[94p]

    　　女人漏下赤白，月经不调，灸交信[交信　《千金》卷四赤白带下崩中漏下作「交仪」。]三十壮，穴在内踝上五寸。　　女人漏下赤白，灸营池四穴三十壮，穴在内踝前后两边池中脉上，一名阴阳是[一名阴阳是　原作「一本是荣池」，据《千金》卷四赤白带下崩中漏下改。]。　　女人漏下赤白，四肢酸削，灸漏阴三十壮，穴在内踝下五分微动脚脉上。　　女人漏下赤白，泄注，灸阴阳随年壮，三报，穴在足拇趾下屈里长头白肉际。　　《李杲十书》曰：妇人赤白带，三阴交刺入五分，灸三十壮。　　又法：漏阴刺入五分，灸三十壮，穴在内踝下五分，微有动脉。　　朱震亨《心法》曰：妇人得子，多变成白水淋漓而下，经久，身面虚肿，刺阴谷入二寸半。　　又法：绝骨穴刺入二寸半。[95p]

    Women experiencing red and white discharge with irregular menstruation should undergo moxibustion at the Jiao Xin point, using thirty doses, located five inches above the inner ankle.

    For women with red and white discharge, moxibustion should be done at the Ying Chi point, using thirty doses, with the point located on both sides of the ankle along the pulse. This point is also known as Yin Yang.

    In cases of red and white discharge accompanied by weakness in the limbs, moxibustion should be applied to the Lou Yin point with thirty doses, located five minutes below the inner ankle over a slight pulse.

    For women with red and white discharge and excessive fluid loss, moxibustion should be done at the Yin Yang point according to the seasonal pattern, using three doses, located at the bend of the big toe by the long head of the pale flesh.

    According to the "Ten Books of Li Gao," for women with red and white discharge, needle the San Yin Jiao point to a depth of half an inch and apply thirty doses of moxibustion.

    Another method for the Lou Yin point is to needle to a depth of half an inch, with thirty doses of moxibustion, located five minutes below the inner ankle where there is a slight pulse.

    Zhu Zhenheng's "Heart Method" states that when women conceive, it often results in a watery discharge for an extended period. This can cause swelling and a void state in the body; needle the Yin Gu point to a depth of two and a half inches.

    Additionally, it is advised to needle the Jue Gu point to a depth of two and a half inches.[95p]

    　　又法：如喘满，刺鱼际穴透太渊穴，左右共四十九呼，治肺经水气极妙。　　《证治准绳》曰：赤白带，刺中极入二寸半，赤泻白补；白环俞一寸半，泻六吸，补一吸。　　又法：气海、中极、白环俞三穴不效，取阳交穴，补多泻少，灸七壮；又取三阴交。　　又法：下白带不已，渐渐如蛊，取气海穴六分，中极、委中二穴各五分。赤带如法。　　又法：下白带不已，渐渐如蛊，取曲骨、承阴二穴各七分；中极六分，穴在两旁柱骨下。赤带如法。　　又法：四花穴，治赤白带如神。[96p]

    Another method: For excessive喘 (panting), needle the fish joint point and penetrate the Taiyuan point, a total of forty-nine breaths on both sides, to treat the lung meridian's water energy extremely well. The "Principles of Diagnosis and Treatment" states: For red and white discharge, needle the center's extreme to two and a half inches deep, reduce with red and tonify with white; for the Baihuanyu point, one and a half inches deep, reduce six times and tonify once. Another method: If the points Qihai, Zhongji, and Baihuanyu are ineffective, use the Yangjiao point, tonifying more and reducing less, with moxibustion seven times; also take the Sanyinjiao point. Another method: If white discharge persists, gradually like a worm, take the Qihai point at six-tenths, and the Zhongji and Weizhong points at five-tenths each. Treat red discharge as per the method. Another method: If white discharge persists, gradually like a worm, take the Qugu and Chengyin points at seven-tenths each; Zhongji at six-tenths, with the points located beneath the lateral bones. Treat red discharge as per the method. Another method: The four flowers point is remarkably effective for treating red and white discharge.[96p]

    　　　　　医案

    　　《儒门事亲》曰：息城李左衙之妻，病白带如水，窈漏中绵绵不绝，秽臭之气不可近，面黄食减，已三年矣。诸医皆云积冷，起石、硫黄、姜、附之药，重重燥补，污水转多，常以袽日易数次。或用一药，以木炭十斤，置药在坩锅中，盐泥封固，三日三夜，炭火不绝，烧令通赤，名曰水龙丹、服至数升，污水弥甚，灼艾烧针，三年之间，不可胜数。戴人断之曰：此带浊水，本热乘太阳经，其寒水不可胜如此也。夫水自高而趋下，宜先绝其上源。乃涌痰水二三升，次日下污水十余行，三遍汗出周身，至明旦，病人云：污已不下矣。次用寒凉之剂，服及半载，产一子。《内经》曰：少腹冤热，溲出白液。带之为病，溶溶然若坐水中。故治带下同治湿法泻利，皆宜逐水利小溲，勿以赤为热，白为寒。今代刘河间书中，言之详矣。[97p]

    Medical Case

    In "Confucian Teachings on Filial Piety," it is stated: The wife of Li Zuoya from Xicheng suffered from a discharge like water, continuous and unending, with an unbearable foul odor. She had a pale complexion and had reduced her food intake for three years. The physicians all diagnosed her condition as due to accumulated cold. They prescribed various herbs including stone, sulfur, ginger, and others, aiming to dry and replenish her, but the discharge only increased. She frequently changed her clothes due to the condition.

    One remedy suggested involved taking ten pounds of charcoal, placing the herbs in a crucible, sealing it with salt mud, and maintaining continuous charcoal heat for three days and nights until it turned completely red, thus creating a medicine known as Water Dragon Pill, which she took in large quantities, but the discharges worsened. Cautiously, the physician Dairen concluded that this was a case of severe dampness caused by heat impacting the channels of the sun; that is, the cold water was overwhelming. Since water flows downward from high to low, it is essential to cut off the source above.

    The patient released two to three liters of thick fluid, and the next day expelled more than ten streams of muddy water. After three rounds of vigorous sweating, by dawn, the patient reported that the foul discharge had ceased. Subsequently, she was given a cold and cooling remedy, and after half a year, she gave birth to a son. The "Inner Canon" states that when there is heat in the lower abdomen, white fluid is discharged. The condition resembles sitting in water. Therefore, treating abnormal discharges is similar to treating dampness, requiring the expulsion of water and facilitating urination. Do not regard red as hot and white as cold. Liu Hejian's writings elaborate on this matter thoroughly.[97p]

    　　顷顿丘一妇人，病带下连绵不绝，白物或来已三年矣，命予脉之。诊其两手，脉俱滑大而有力，得六七至，常上热口干眩运，时呕酢水。余知其实有寒痰在胸中，以瓜蒂散吐出冷痰二三升，皆酢水也，间如黄涎，状如烂胶；次以浆粥养其胃气；又次用导水、禹功以泻其下；然后以淡剂渗泄之药利其水道，不数日而愈。
    　　《丹溪心法》曰：胡安人患白带下，月经甚多，食少倦怠，面黄，经中有如血块者，有如筋膜者，与参、朮等补血气，调脾胃；后诸证皆退，惟带未止，以樗皮丸主之而愈。
    　　《薛氏医案》曰：一孀妇腹胀胁痛，内热晡热，月经不调，肢体酸麻，不时吐痰；或用清气化痰之药，喉间不利，带下青黄，腹胁膨胀；又用行气之剂，胸膈不利，肢体如麻。此乃郁怒伤损肝脾，朝用归脾汤以解脾郁、生脾气，夕用加味逍遥散以生肝血、清肝火，百余剂而愈。[98p]

    Recently, there was a woman in Dongqiu who suffered from continuous vaginal discharge, a white fluid, for three years. I was asked to take her pulse. Upon diagnosing her wrists, the pulses felt smooth, large, and strong, with six or seven beats, and she often experienced heat in her body, dry mouth, dizziness, and occasional vomiting of sour fluid. I suspected she had cold phlegm in her chest, and used a remedy to expel cold phlegm, yielding two to three liters of fluid, mostly sour water, with some resembling yellow saliva and appearing like rotting glue. Next, I employed congee to nourish her stomach qi, then used methods to guide water and apply draining techniques to clear her lower body. After administering diuretic medicines that promote fluid drainage for several days, she was cured.

    In the "Danxi Heart Methods," it is stated: A Hu'an woman suffers from excessive vaginal discharge, abundant menstrual flow, little appetite, fatigue, a pale face, and blood-like clots or membranous substances in her menstruation. I recommended using ginseng, atractylodes, and other tonics to replenish blood and qi, balancing the spleen and stomach; eventually, all symptoms diminished, but the discharge persisted, for which I prescribed Chupi Pills, leading to her recovery.

    According to "Xue's Medical Cases," one widowed woman presented with abdominal distension and pain in her sides, internal heat, afternoon fevers, irregular menstruation, and limbs that felt sore and numb, with sporadic phlegm. Initially, I used medicines to clear qi and transform phlegm, but her throat felt constricted, and she had a bluish-yellow discharge with abdominal distension. When I applied agents to move qi, her chest felt uncomfortably full, and her limbs remained numb. This condition was due to emotional distress harming her liver and spleen. I administered Guizhi Spleen Decoction in the morning to relieve spleen depression and strengthen spleen qi, followed by Jiawei Xiaoyao Powder in the evening to nourish liver blood and clear liver fire. After over a hundred doses, she was cured.[98p]

    　　一妇人头运吐痰，胸满气喘，得食稍缓，苦于白带二十余年矣，诸药不应，此气虚而痰饮也，痰饮愈而带自愈。遂朝用六君子汤，夕用六味地黄丸，不一月而验。
    　　一妇人耳鸣胸痞，内热口干，喉中若有核，吞吐不利，月经不调，兼之带下，余以为肝脾郁结，用归脾汤加半夏、山栀、升麻、柴胡，间以四七汤下白丸子而愈。
    　　一妇人吞酸饱满，食少便泄，月经不调，服清气化痰丸，两膝渐肿，寒热往来，带下黄白，面痿体倦，此脾胃俱虚，湿痰下注，用补中益气倍用参、朮，加茯苓、半夏、炮姜而愈。
    　　一妇人带下，四肢无力，余曰：四肢者土也，此脾胃虚弱，湿痰下注，以补中益气、济生归脾二药治之而愈。
    　　一妇人带下黄白，怒则胸膈不利，饮食少思，或用消导利气之药，痰喘胸满，大便下血。余曰：此因脾气亏损，不能摄血归源，用补中益气加茯苓、半夏、炮姜四剂顿减，又用八珍加柴胡、山栀而痊。[99p]

    A woman experienced coughing and phlegm, with a feeling of fullness in the chest and wheezing. She found some relief after eating but suffered from excessive discharge for over twenty years, unresponsive to various medications. This was due to deficiency of qi and phlegm. As the phlegm decreased, the discharge resolved itself. Therefore, she took Liu Jun Zi Tang in the morning and Liu Wei Di Huang Wan in the evening, and within a month, she saw improvement.

    Another woman had tinnitus and a feeling of fullness in the chest, with internal heat and dry mouth. She felt as though there was a lump in her throat, and swallowing was difficult. Her menstrual cycles were irregular, and she also had discharge. I diagnosed her with liver and spleen stagnation and prescribed Gui Pi Tang, adding Ban Xia, Shan Zhi, Sheng Ma, and Chai Hu. Alternating with Si Qi Tang and taking white pills, she recovered.

    A different woman experienced sourness in her throat, fullness after eating, a reduced appetite, and diarrhea. Her menstrual cycle was irregular. She took Qing Qi Hua Tan Wan, but then her knees swelled gradually, with alternating chills and fever, yellow-white discharge, facial weakness, and body fatigue. This indicated deficiency in both spleen and stomach, with damp phlegm downward. I used Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang, increasing the amount of Ren Shen and Bai Zhu, and added Fu Ling, Ban Xia, and Pao Jiang, leading to her recovery.

    Another woman had discharge and weakness in her limbs. I stated: "The limbs correspond to the earth element." This indicated weakness in the spleen and stomach, with damp phlegm downward. I treated her with Bu Zhong Yi Qi and Ji Sheng Gui Pi, resulting in her recovery.

    Lastly, a woman had yellow-white discharge, and when angry, she felt obstructed in the chest. She had reduced appetite and thought processes. I considered using herbs to disperse and regulate qi, yet she experienced phlegm, chest fullness, and bloody stools. I diagnosed this as due to deficiency of spleen qi, preventing it from absorbing and returning blood to the source. I used Bu Zhong Yi Qi, adding Fu Ling, Ban Xia, and Pao Jiang in four doses, and also added Ba Zhen Tang with Chai Hu and Shan Zhi, leading to her healing.[99p]

    　　一妇人年逾六十，内热口干，劳则头运吐痰带下，或用化痰行气，前证益甚，饮食益少，肢体或麻；服袪风化痰之剂，肢体常麻，手足或冷或热，日渐消瘦。余曰：此证属脾气虚弱而不能生肺，袪风之剂，复损诸经也，当滋化源。遂用补中益气加茯苓、半夏、炮姜二十余剂，脾气渐复，饮食渐加，诸证顿愈。
    　　《证治准绳》曰：雪翁妻，年三十余，十八胎九殇八夭，曾因事惊忧过甚，遂昏昏不省人事，口唇舌皆疮，或至封喉，下部虚脱，白带如注，如此四十余日，或时少醒，至欲自缢，自悲不能堪医。或投凉剂解其上，则下部疾愈甚；或投热剂，及以汤药熏蒸其下，则热运欲绝。四弟还脉之，始知为亡阳证也，急以盐煮大附子九钱为君，制以薄荷、防风，佐以姜、桂、芎、归之属，水煎入井冰冷与之，未尽剂，鼾呼熟睡通宵，觉即能识人。时止一嗣子二女，相抱痛哭，疏戚皆悲。[100p]

    A woman over sixty years old experienced internal heat and dry mouth. When fatigued, she had headaches, phlegm, and discharge. Attempts to resolve phlegm and promote Qi made her symptoms worse, leading to reduced appetite and occasional numbness in her limbs. After taking remedies to dispel wind and resolve phlegm, she continued to feel numbness in her limbs, with her hands and feet alternating between being cold and hot, and she gradually became emaciated. I said: This condition is due to weak spleen Qi, which cannot nourish the lungs. The wind-dispelling remedies further harm the meridians, so it is necessary to nourish the source of digestion. I then prescribed over twenty doses of a formula to tonify the middle and augment Qi, adding Poria, Pinellia, and roasted ginger. Her spleen Qi gradually improved, her appetite increased, and all symptoms quickly resolved.

    The "Principles of Diagnosis and Treatment" states: The wife of Xue Weng, aged over thirty, had eighteen pregnancies, with nine stillbirths and eight deaths in infancy. After being overly shocked and worried due to an event, she became confused and unaware of her surroundings, with sores on her mouth, lips, and tongue. At times, she nearly choked, suffering from lower body weakness and a profuse white discharge for over forty days. Occasionally, she became slightly aware, to the point of wanting to hang herself, feeling unable to bear the illness. When some cold remedies were given to address her upper symptoms, her lower condition worsened. Attempts to use hot remedies and steam treatments on her lower body only aggravated the heat. Four of her brothers checked her pulse and realized it was a case of Yang deficiency. In urgency, they prepared nine qian of processed Aconite boiled with salt as the main ingredient, with mint and Saposhnikovia as assistants, along with ginger, cinnamon, Chuanxiong, and angelica. They decocted it with cool spring water and gave it to her. After just a few doses, she fell into a deep sleep, breathing steadily through the night, and upon waking, she could recognize people. At that time, she had one son and two daughters, who held onto each other and wept, with everyone filled with sorrow.[100p]

    执友赵宪长惊曰：君何术也？弟曰：方书有之，假对假、真对真耳。上乃假热，故以假冷之药从之：下乃真冷，故以真热之药反之，斯上下和而病解矣。继后主以女金丹，错综以二三方，不但去其疾，且调治元气。庚午生一子，壬申生一子。去年又患疟疾十三月，亦主以养元气，调生气；待饮食大进，然后劫以毒药，吐下块物甚多，投以附子汤三钱而愈。不责效旦暮间。其用女金丹即胜金丸也，得之异人。倍加香附而视气血之偏者，又加姜黄、条芩倍川芎之属，取效甚多。予念无子者往往有之，翻思予得子之难，其苦何如？乃次第录其方，并女金丹以济人。[101p]

    Zhao Xianchang, a close friend, exclaimed: "What technique is this?" The disciple replied: "It is mentioned in the medical texts; we use false against false and true against true. Thus, since the upper part is falsely hot, we treat it with a false cold medicine; since the lower part is truly cold, we counter it with a truly hot medicine. This way, the upper and lower parts harmonize and the illness resolves."

    Following the former ruler, I used a female elixir of gold and combined it with various prescriptions, which not only cured the ailments but also balanced the vital energy. In the year of Gengwu, a son was born, and in Ren Shen, another son was born. Last year, I also suffered from intermittent fever for thirteen months; I relied on nourishing the vital energy and regulating the life force. After a substantial intake of food, I then countered it with toxic medicine, resulting in significant purging with much vomit and stool. Afterwards, I administered three qian of aconite soup and he recovered.

    Effectiveness was not tied to the morning or evening. The elixir used was indeed superior to the golden pills obtained from extraordinary sources. By increasing the amount of cyperus and examining the imbalances of qi and blood, I also added turmeric and various herbs akin to gentian, which yielded significant results.

    I pondered that those without children often face such hardships, and reflecting on how difficult it is for me to have children, I felt the bitterness of it. Thus, I sequentially documented my methods, including the female elixir of gold, to assist others.[101p]

    　　陶遵道外姑。年七十，形瘦善啖，病白带，食前，姜汤吞大补九五十丸一二次，午膳后又临卧时，各与小胃丹十五丸愈。
    　　一妇人因产后虚寒，呕恶不食，腹痛如割，时作寒热，复出盗汗，瘦悴骨立，脐腹之左，结成硬块，其大如掌，冰冷，虽盛暑，此处独无汗，每块微动则痛不可忍，百药治不效。梦中忽有人授以艾煎丸方，因服之，恶心寒热盗汗辄止，尽一料遂平复，独血块如故；服至五六料，其块自融化而出如鱼冻。
    [102p]

    Tao Zundao's external aunt, aged seventy, was slender and had a good appetite. She suffered from a white discharge and, before meals, would take ginger soup and swallow large doses of pills, around ninety to a hundred, one to two times. After lunch, when resting, she would take fifteen small stomach pills and was cured.

    A woman, after childbirth, experienced weakness from cold, nausea, inability to eat, and abdominal pain as if being cut. She had intermittent chills and fever, excessive sweating at night, was emaciated and bony, with a hard mass the size of a palm on the left side of her navel, which was cool to the touch. Despite the hot summer, there was no sweating in that area, and any movement caused unbearable pain. Many remedies had no effect. In a dream, someone suddenly handed her a recipe for moxa pill decoction. After taking it, her nausea, chills, and night sweat ceased, and after consuming one dose, she returned to normal, but the blood clot remained unchanged. After taking five or six doses, the mass naturally dissolved and emerged like fish gelatin.[102p]
